class=\"entry-header page-header\">\n\n\t\t\t<h1 class=\"entry-title \">Under the Heel of the Rothschilds</h1>\n\n\t\t\t<div class=\"entry-meta\">\n\t\t\t\t<span class=\"byline\"> <i class=\"fa fa-user fa-2x\"></i> <span class=\"author vcard\"><a class=\"url fn n\" href=\"https://www.darkmoon.me/author/admin/\">Admin</a></span></span><span class=\"posted-on\"><i class=\"fa fa-calendar\"></i> <a href=\"https://www.darkmoon.me/2017/under-the-heel-of-the-rothschilds/\" rel=\"bookmark\"><time class=\"entry-date published\" datetime=\"2017-02-25T09:06:29+00:00\">February 25, 2017</time><time class=\"updated\" datetime=\"2017-02-25T09:50:20+00:00\">February 25, 2017</time></a></span>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<span class=\"cat-links\"><i class=\"fa fa-folder-open-o\"></i>\n\t\t\t\t\t <a href=\"https://www.darkmoon.me/category/other-writers/\" rel=\"category tag\">Other Writers</a>\t\t\t\t</span>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t</div><!-- .entry-meta -->\n\t\t</header><!-- .entry-header -->\n\n\t\t<div class=\"entry-content\">\n\t\t\t<p style=\"text-align: center;\"><strong>By <span style=\"color: #800000;\"><em>ARCH STANTON</em></span></strong></p>\n<h4 style=\"text-align: left;\"><img class=\"aligncenter size-large wp-image-61063\" src=\"https://www.darkmoon.me/uploads/648x322xmaxresdefault-10-1024x509.jpg.pagespeed.ic.0Yw4pMeUtm.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"648\" height=\"322\" srcset=\"https://www.darkmoon.me/uploads/maxresdefault-10-1024x509.jpg 1024w, https://www.darkmoon.me/uploads/maxresdefault-10-150x75.jpg 150w, https://www.darkmoon.me/uploads/maxresdefault-10-300x149.jpg 300w, https://www.darkmoon.me/uploads/maxresdefault-10-768x382.jpg 768w, https://www.darkmoon.me/uploads/maxresdefault-10-600x298.jpg 600w, https://www.darkmoon.me/uploads/maxresdefault-10.jpg 1504w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 648px) 100vw, 648px\"/></h4>\n<h3 style=\"text-align: center;\"><span style=\"color: #800000;\">UNDER \u00a0THE \u00a0HEEL \u00a0OF \u00a0THE \u00a0ROTHSCHILDS</span></h3>\n<h5 style=\"text-align: center;\">&#8220;And one man, Donald Trump, is supposed to reverse all this?&#8221;<br/>\n\u2014 Arch Stanton</h5>\n<p><strong>That America is on &#8220;life support&#8221; has been clear for a long time\u2014in fact, ever since the Swinging Sixties and the end of the Vietnam war. America\u2019s rapidly deteriorating condition of the late seventies is what led to my search for what happened to the promise of &#8220;the American dream\u201d.</strong><br/>\n<span id=\"more-61003\"></span></p>\n<p>What I cannot comprehend is all this wringing of hands, rending of garments and gnashing of teeth. It\u2019s like that old scorpion story. Didn&#8217;t America know what was going on <em>before</em> Trump was elected to ride on its back? Apparently not.</p>\n<p>Observe: the Rothschilds consolidated their European holdings of wealth and power by the late 1700s. By the turn of that century, they virtually owned, and most certainly controlled Britain, the sole superpower of the day, a global power on whose colonial holdings &#8220;the sun never set.\u201d</p>\n<p><img class=\"aligncenter wp-image-57823\" src=\"https://www.darkmoon.me/uploads/642x406xRothschilds.jpg.pagespeed.ic.klRHOhfyN_.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"642\" height=\"406\" srcset=\"https://www.darkmoon.me/uploads/Rothschilds.jpg 753w, https://www.darkmoon.me/uploads/Rothschilds-150x95.jpg 150w, https://www.darkmoon.me/uploads/Rothschilds-300x190.jpg 300w, https://www.darkmoon.me/uploads/Rothschilds-600x380.jpg 600w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 642px) 100vw, 642px\"/></p>\n<p>The Rothschilds also exercised considerable influence over the outcome of the Napoleonic wars (1803-1815) that served to strangle the rise of another potential superpower: France. The financial power of the Rothschilds had originally been based in France, but when Napoleon began to resist their economic plans for his country, the Rothschilds diverted money to Britain and stirred up conflict between Britain and its traditional enemy France. The result: the demise of Napoleonic power at the battle of Waterloo (1815).</p>\n<p>From that point on, Rothschild power grew by leaps and bounds. They played a critical part in fomenting and influencing the American revolution (1765-1783), the war of 1812 between America and Britain, the Mexican-American war of the late 1840s, and the American \u201cCivil War\u201d of 1861-1865.</p>\n<p>By this time, the Rothschilds had begun expanding their parasitical power base to the \u201cNew world.\u201d These wars reflected their emerging interest in America and their gradual abandonment of Britain as their center of power. With the Jews it has always been about war, war, war and more war. Since the day Jews fabricated their Torah, it\u2019s always been about bloody war.</p>\n<p>By the end of the 19th century, the Rothschilds had begun consolidating their control over America. Around the same time, a small portion of their global plan was unveiled by the sensational publication \u00a0of the <em>Protocols of the Elders of Zion </em>(1903), since conveniently dismissed as a &#8220;forgery&#8221;.</p>\n<p>A scant twelve years after the new century began, the Rothschilds&#8217; full economic control over America was finally accomplished with the enactment of the Federal Reserve Act (December 1913). Within seven months of that Act, the world was at war, dragging America (with its massive army of two million troops) into the bloodshed. This was in April, 1917.</p>\n<p>The Federal Reserve act was the very same Br\u2019er Rabbit scheme replayed with Trump\u2019s election.</p>\n<p>Jewish economic influence then fomented two of the most murderous wars in history, first one in 1914 and then a second in 1939, a scant quarter of a century after the first major killing campaign. From the very beginning of the century, brush wars raged throughout the century in places like the Philippines and South America.</p>\n<p><img class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-61004\" src=\"https://www.darkmoon.me/uploads/xJUDEA-DECLARES-WAR-ON-GERMANY.jpg.pagespeed.ic._wzy84BuRG.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"640\" height=\"463\" srcset=\"https://www.darkmoon.me/uploads/JUDEA-DECLARES-WAR-ON-GERMANY.jpg 640w, https://www.darkmoon.me/uploads/JUDEA-DECLARES-WAR-ON-GERMANY-150x109.jpg 150w, https://www.darkmoon.me/uploads/JUDEA-DECLARES-WAR-ON-GERMANY-300x217.jpg 300w, https://www.darkmoon.me/uploads/JUDEA-DECLARES-WAR-ON-GERMANY-600x434.jpg 600w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 640px) 100vw, 640px\"/></p>\n<blockquote><p><strong>In spite of this headline in a major newspaper in March 1933, you will still hear Jews hotly deny that they had anything to do with starting WWII. Regarded as an &#8220;anti-Semitic canard&#8221;, any public statement\u00a0along the lines that Jews helped to kickstart the bloodbath of WWII can lead to loss of employment, social ostracism and other dreadful sanctions. The truth is no defense.\u00a0</strong></p></blockquote>\n<p>Just after the midpoint of the century\u2019s global wars came the &#8220;sexual revolution\u201d of the 1960s. This was a thinly disguised, Jewish, cultural Marxist revolution that served to destroy American culture, reducing it to one of ignorant, stupid, rutting beasts that have now taken over the country, willingly marching in \u00a0lockstep behind the Jews\u2019 unanimous cry for more warring bloodshed around the planet.</p>\n<p>So there should not be the slightest surprise in finding the world in its present uproar, with war once again on the horizon. Thanks to the Jews\u2019 destabilizing wars and revolutions, almost all the Near East has been destabilized and destroyed. The secondary effect of this destruction has been the unrestricted flooding of Europe with immigrants, thereby destabilizing and destroying most of Europe and its different cultures.</p>\n<p>You are naturally not allowed to say that the Jews had anything to do with the &#8220;migrant crisis&#8221;\u2014unless of course you happen to be an extraordinarily foolish Jew who lets the cat out of the bag by openly blabbing about Jewish responsibility for this major catastrophe:</p>\n<h2 style=\"text-align: center;\"><span style=\"color: #0000ff;\"><a style=\"color: #0000ff;\" href=\"https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=8ERmOpZrKtw\">36-SECOND VIDEO </a></span></h2>\n<p>Thanks to Jewish economic control that enabled them to eviscerate American manufacturing and industry\u2014with a tidy profit to Jewish middle-men\u2014America is now fully dependent on global trade for its survival. America can no longer survive without a constant infusion of foreign trade that is completely controlled by Jewish economic policy.</p>\n<p>And one man, Donald Trump, is supposed to reverse all this?</p>\n<p>How can anyone be so naive as to believe that any one person, or even a small group of people, could ever reverse this continuous parade of long-standing historical trends that began with the Rothschilds&#8217; accumulation of a major portion of the world\u2019s wealth?</p>\n<p>This should be especially obvious considering Jews have all the wealth to fund their agenda with, while the goyim are left with little more than angry words.</p>\n<p style=\"line-height: 18.0pt; background: white; margin: 0in 0in 7.5pt 0in;\"><strong><span style=\"font-family: 'Libre Baskerville','serif'; color: #222222;\"><em>LD comments:</em> I revealed in a <a href=\"http://www.thetruthseeker.co.uk/?p=146654\">recent article</a> that the Rothschild family is widely reported to own\u00a0</span><span style=\"font-family: 'Libre Baskerville','serif'; color: #222222;\">as much as the rest of the world\u2019s 7.5 billion people put together, if not\u00a0</span><span style=\"font-family: 'Libre Baskerville','serif'; color: #222222;\">more:</span></strong></p>\n<blockquote>\n<p style=\"line-height: 18.0pt; background: white; box-sizing: border-box; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; widows: 2; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; word-spacing: 0px; margin: 0in 0in 7.5pt 0in;\"><strong><span style=\"font-family: 'Libre Baskerville','serif'; color: #222222;\">Jews make up 11% of the world\u2019s billionaires, so the Jews are doing exceptionally well given that they make up only 0.2% of the world\u2019s population. (<span style=\"font-family: 'Libre Baskerville','serif';\"><a style=\"box-sizing: border-box; transition: all 0.3s;\" href=\"http://takimag.com/article/jewish_wealth_by_the_numbers_steve_sailer/print#axzz4Wg7uwcsr\"><span style=\"color: #1f63b5; text-decoration: none; text-underline: none;\">Source</span></a></span>)</span></strong></p>\n<p style=\"line-height: 18.0pt; background: white; box-sizing: border-box; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; widows: 2; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; word-spacing: 0px; margin: 0in 0in 7.5pt 0in;\"><strong><span style=\"font-family: 'Libre Baskerville','serif'; color: #222222;\">Jews make up only 2% of America\u2019s population; but according to a recent\u00a0<em style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"font-family: 'Libre Baskerville','serif';\">Forbes Israel</span></em>\u00a0list, they make up a whopping 24% of American billionaires. Out of 442 US billionaires, 105 were Jews. (<span style=\"font-family: 'Libre Baskerville','serif';\"><a style=\"box-sizing: border-box; transition: all 0.3s;\" href=\"http://takimag.com/article/jewish_wealth_by_the_numbers_steve_sailer/print#axzz4Wg7uwcsr\"><span style=\"color: #1f63b5; text-decoration: none; text-underline: none;\">Source</span></a></span>). With such enormous wealth concentrated in the hands of American Jews, is it any wonder they own the mass media and major corporations as well as have huge reserves left over for the bribery and corruption of American politicians?</span></strong></p>\n<p style=\"line-height: 18.0pt; background: white; box-sizing: border-box; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; widows: 2; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; word-spacing: 0px; margin: 0in 0in 7.5pt 0in;\"><strong><span style=\"font-family: 'Libre Baskerville','serif'; color: #222222;\">The statement that the Rothschild family alone owns FIVE times as much as the combined wealth of the world\u2019s EIGHT wealthiest billionaires in the world combined, is obviously calculated to create unbounded astonishment at the vast wealth of the Rothschilds. And yet to many astute observers the statement will be seen as a deliberate\u00a0<em style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"font-family: 'Libre Baskerville','serif';\">underestimate</span></em>\u00a0of Rothschild wealth. </span></strong></p>\n<p style=\"line-height: 18.0pt; background: white; box-sizing: border-box; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; widows: 2; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; word-spacing: 0px; margin: 0in 0in 7.5pt 0in;\"><strong><span style=\"font-family: 'Libre Baskerville','serif'; color: #222222;\">It is widely known\u2014or at any rate, suspected\u2014that the Rothschilds own roughly $500 TRILLION. This amounts to exactly half of the $1000 trillion owned by the rest of the world\u2019s 7.5 billion population. (See\u00a0<span style=\"font-family: 'Libre Baskerville','serif';\"><span style=\"color: #1f63b5; text-decoration: none; text-underline: none;\"><a style=\"box-sizing: border-box; transition: all 0.3s;\" href=\"https://www.darkmoon.me/2016/the-fabulous-wealth-of-the-rothschilds-3-minute-video/\">here</a></span></span>)</span></strong></p>\n<p style=\"line-height: 18.0pt; background: white; box-sizing: border-box; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; orphans: 2; text-align: start; widows: 2; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; word-spacing: 0px; margin: 0in 0in 7.5pt 0in;\"><strong>[LD]</strong></p>\n</blockquote>\n<p><strong>ARCH \u00a0STANTON</strong><em>\u00a0 (continues)</em><strong> :</strong>\u00a0 It must surely be obvious to all that the world is running straight, narrow and true on rails paid for by Rothschild money. What I see in all this brouhaha about Donald Trump is exactly what was to be expected, <em>i.e.,</em> another Jewish dog-and-pony show intended to occupy the public while other, far more critical, events pass unnoticed.</p>\n<p>This is exactly the way Jews have been playing the deception game since the days of the Old Testament when they marched around Jericho singing, shouting and blowing horns to disguise their sappers undermining Jericho\u2019s fortifying walls.</p>\n<p>Jews pride themselves on their magical acumen. Magicians base their act on deception. Hey, look at what <em>this</em> hand is doing! \u2014so you don&#8217;t notice what the <em>other</em> hand is up to! This is the game being enacted now in the Trump charade, <em>n\u2019est-ce pas?</em></p>\n<p>From the beginning of their rise to a global, economic power, the Rothschilds and their Jewish henchmen have been calling the shots like the global criminal mafia they have always been. Whether the world recognizes this and takes action to excise this virulent, diseased parasite or suffer the terminal consequences of watching the big game on television while the world goes up in flames, remains to be seen.</p>\n<p>If past performance is an indication of future outcome, the world can expect a nuclear war any time soon. So far, Jews have a better performance record at creating war then a Warren Buffet fund has at creating wealth.</p>\n<p>Why complicate this issue when it&#8217;s really simple?</p>\n<p>The American dream, thanks to the machinations of the Rothschilds and their minions, has now morphed into a full-blown nightmare.</p>\n<!-- Simple Share Buttons Adder (6.3.4) simplesharebuttons.com --><div class=\"ssba ssba-wrap\"><div style=\"text-align:center\">Like this? rel=\"nofollow\">http://www.bis.org/about/member_cb.htm</a></p>\n<p> Even Iceland.. \ud83d\ude42</p>\n<p>24.02.2017<br/>\nNew payment systems </p>\n<p>Yesterday the Central Bank of Iceland signed an agreement with Italian software provider SIA concerning the purchase and implementation of new software for interbank payments in Iceland. The new systems will supersede the current real-time gross settlement (RTGS) and netting systems, which have been in use since 2001.</p>\n<p>The RTGS system is a payment system that handles the settlement of all payment instructions between participants (i.e., financial institutions) in amounts of 10 million Icelandic kr\u00f3nur or more. The retail netting system is a payment and settlement system for monetary transactions involving amounts less than 10 m.kr. Total turnover in Icelandic interbank payment intermediation systems amounted to about 21,000 billion kr\u00f3nur in 2016.<br/>\n<a href=\"http://www.cb.is/default.aspx?pageid=d97dc9fd-0493-11e5-93fa-005056bc0bdb\" rel=\"nofollow\">http://www.cb.is/default.aspx?pageid=d97dc9fd-0493-11e5-93fa-005056bc0bdb</a></p>\n\t\t\t\t</div><!-- .comment-content -->\n\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t</article><!-- .comment-body -->\n</li><!-- resident sinologist at Darkmoon, permit me to give a quick Chinese history lesson that may prove instructive in overthrowing our present Jewish Oligarchs. </p>\n<p>From Wikipedia&#8217;s entry for &#8220;<a href=\"https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Queue_(hairstyle)\" rel=\"nofollow\">Queue</a>&#8220;: </p>\n<blockquote><p>The queue was a specifically male hairstyle worn by the Manchu people from central Manchuria and later imposed on the Han Chinese during the Qing dynasty.[3][4][5] The hair on the front of the head was shaved off above the temples every ten days and the remainder of the hair was braided into a long braid.[6]</p>\n<p>The Manchu hairstyle was forcefully introduced to Han Chinese in the early 17th century during the Manchu conquest of China. Nurhaci of the Aisin Gioro clan declared the establishment of the Later Jin dynasty, later becoming the Qing dynasty of China, after Ming dynasty forces in Liaodong defected to his side. The Ming general of Fushun, Li Yongfang, defected to Nurhaci after Nurhaci promised him rewards, titles, and Nurhaci&#8217;s own granddaughter in marriage. Other Han Chinese generals in Liaodong proceeded to defect with their armies to Nurhaci and were given women from the Aisin Gioro family in marriage. Once firmly in power, Nurhaci commanded all men in the areas he conquered to adopt the Manchu hairstyle.</p>\n<p><strong>The Manchu hairstyle signified Han submission to Qing rule, and also aided the Manchu identification of those Han who refused to accept Qing dynasty domination.</strong></p>\n<p>The hairstyle was compulsory for all males and the penalty for non-compliance was execution for treason. In the early 1910s, after the fall of the Qing dynasty, the Chinese no longer had to wear the Manchu queue. While some, such as Zhang Xun, still did so as a tradition, most of them abandoned it after the last Emperor of China, Puyi, cut his queue in 1922.[7]</p></blockquote>\n<p>What does all this have to do with the Rothschilds the reader may ask? The family had three popes (Leo X \u2013 pictured above, Clement VII, and Leo XI), numerous rulers of Florence &#8211; notably Lorenzo the Magnificent, patron of some of the most famous works of Renaissance art &#8211; and later members of the French and English royalty. Like other signore families they dominated their city\u2019s government. They were able to bring Florence under their family\u2019s power, allowing for an environment where art and humanism could flourish. </p>\n<p>The Medici Family led the birth of the Italian Renaissance along with the other great signore families of Italy such as the Visconti and Sforza families of Milan, the Este of Ferrara, and the Gonzaga of Mantua. </p>\n<p>The Medici Bank was one of the most prosperous and most respected in Europe. victim feminism, the gay rights movement, the invented statistics, the rewritten history, the lies, the demands, all the rest of it \u2013 where does it come from? For the first time in our history, Americans have to be fearful of what they say, of what they write, and of what they think. They have to be afraid of using the wrong word, a word denounced as offensive or insensitive, or racist, sexist, or homophobic. We have seen other countries, particularly in this century, where this has been the case. And we have always regarded them with a mixture of pity, and to be truthful, some amusement, because it has struck us as so strange that people would allow a situation to develop where they would be afraid of what words they used. But we now have this situation in this country. We have it primarily on college campuses, but it is spreading throughout the whole society. Were does it come from? What is it? &#8230; If we look at it analytically, if we look at it historically, we quickly find out exactly what it is. Political Correctness is cultural Marxism. It is Marxism translated from economic into cultural terms &#8230; In 1923 in Germany, a think-tank is established that takes on the role of translating Marxism from economic into cultural terms, that creates Political Correctness as we know it today, and essentially it has created the basis for it by the end of the 1930s. This comes about because the very wealthy young son of a millionaire German trader by the name of Felix Weil has become a Marxist and has lots of money to spend &#8230; He endows an institute, associated with Frankfurt University, established in 1923, that was originally supposed to be known as the Institute for Marxism. But the people behind it decided at the beginning that it was not to their advantage to be openly identified as Marxist. The last thing Political Correctness wants is for people to figure out it\u2019s a form of Marxism. class=\"comment-metadata\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t<a href=\"https://www.darkmoon.me/2017/under-the-heel-of-the-rothschilds/#comment-947988\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<time datetime=\"2017-02-26T21:26:58+00:00\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\tFebruary 26, 2017 at 9:26 pm\t\t\t\t\t\t\t</time>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t</a>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t</div><!-- .comment-metadata -->\n\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t</footer><!-- .comment-meta -->\n\n\t\t\t\t<div class=\"comment-content\">\n\t\t\t\t\t<p><strong>JFK QUOTES&#8230;.</strong></p>\n<p>\u201cLet us make it clear that we will never turn our backs on our steadfast friends in Israel, whose adherence to the democratic way must be admired by all friends of freedom.\u201d<br/>\n           (Speech at Eastern Oregon College of Education, November 9, 1959)</p>\n<p>    \u201cWe must formulate, with both imagination and restraint, a new approach to the Middle East \u2014 not pressing our case so hard that the Arabs feel their neutrality and nationalism are threatened &#8230; while at the same time trying to hasten the inevitable Arab acceptance of the permanence of Israel &#8230; We must &#8230; seek a permanent settlement among Arabs and Israelis based not on an armed truce but on mutual self-interest.\u201d<br/>\n           (Near East Report, July 1, 1960)</p>\n<p>    &#8220;Israel was not created in order to disappear\u2014Israel will endure and flourish. It is the child of hope and home of the brave. It can neither be broken by adversity nor demoralized by success. It carries the shield of democracy and it honors the sword of freedom.&#8221;<br/>\n           (Speech to Zionists of America Convention, August 26, 1960)</p>\n<p>    &#8220;This nation, from the time of President Woodrow Wilson, has established and continued a tradition of friendship with Israel because we are committed to all free societies that seek a path to peace and honor individual right. We seek peace and prosperity for all of the Middle East firm in our belief that a new spirit of comity in that important part of the world would serve the highest aspirations and interests of all nations.<br/>\n<strong>In the prophetic spirit of Zionism all free men today look to a better world and in the experience of Zionism we know that it takes courage and perseverance and dedication to achieve it.&#8221;<br/>\n           (Message to Zionist Organization of America Annual Conference, 1962)</p>\n<p>    &#8220;We support the security of both Israel and her neighbors.&#8221;<br/>\n           (Statement on May 8, 1963)</strong></p>\n\t\t\t\t</div><!-- .comment-content -->\n\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t</article><!-- .comment-body -->\n</li><!-- #comment-## -->\n\t\t<li id=\"comment-947992\" class=\"comment odd alt depth-3\">\n\t\t\t<article id=\"div-comment-947992\" class=\"comment-body\">\n\t\t\t\t<footer class=\"comment-meta\">\n\t\t\t\t\t<div class=\"comment-author vcard\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t<img alt='' src='https://secure.gravatar.com/avatar/44949a80a6e3af20b81db86f165130bc?s=60&#038;d=mm&#038;r=pg' srcset='https://secure.gravatar.com/avatar/44949a80a6e3af20b81db86f165130bc?s=120&amp;d=mm&amp;r=pg 2x' class='avatar avatar-60 photo' height='60' width='60'/>\t\t\t\t\t\t<b class=\"fn\">Pat</b> <span class=\"says\">says:</span>\t\t\t\t\t</div><!-- .comment-author -->\n\n\t\t\t\t\t<div class=\"comment-metadata\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t<a href=\"https://www.darkmoon.me/2017/under-the-heel-of-the-rothschilds/#comment-947992\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<time datetime=\"2017-02-26T22:44:19+00:00\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\tFebruary 26, 2017 at 10:44 pm\t\t\t\t\t\t\t</time>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t</a>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t</div><!-- .comment-metadata -->\n\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t</footer><!-- .comment-meta -->\n\n\t\t\t\t<div class=\"comment-content\">\n\t\t\t\t\t<p>I am an equal opportunity basher of US Presidents&#8230;..</p>\n<p><strong>Speech by Senator John F. Kennedy, Zionists of America Convention, Statler Hilton Hotel, New York, NY</strong></p>\n<p>August 26, 1960</p>\n<p><a href=\"http://www.presidency.ucsb.edu/ws/index.php?pid=74217\" rel=\"nofollow\">http://www.presidency.ucsb.edu/ws/index.php?pid=74217</a></p>\n<p>(excerpts)<br/>\nProphecy is a Jewish tradition, and the World Zionist movement, in which all of you have played so important a role, has continued this tradition. It has turned the dreams of its leaders into acts of statesmanship. It has converted the hopes of the Jewish people into concrete facts of life. </p>\n<p>When the first Zionist conference met in 1897, Palestine was a neglected wasteland. A few scattered Jewish colonies had resettled there, but they had come to die in the Holy Land, rather than to make it live again in greatness. Most of the governments of the world were indifferent. </p>\n<p>But now all is changed. Israel became a triumphant and enduring reality exactly 50 years after Theodore Herzl, the prophet of Zionism, had proclaimed the ideal of nationhood. It was the classic case of an ancient dream finding a young leader, for Herzl was then only 37 years of age. </p>\n<p>Perhaps I may be allowed the observation that the Jewish people &#8211; ever since David slew Goliath &#8211; have never considered youth as a barrier to leadership, or measured experience and maturity by mere length of days. </p>\n<p>I first saw Palestine in 1939. There the neglect and ruin left by centuries of Ottoman misrule were slowly being transformed by miracles of labor and sacrifice. But Palestine was still a land of promise in 1939, rather than a land of fulfillment. </p>\n<p>I returned in 1951 to see the grandeur of Israel. In 3 years this new state had opened its doors to 600,000 immigrants and refugees. Even while fighting for its own survival, Israel had given new hope to the persecuted and new dignity to the pattern of Jewish life. I left with the conviction that the United Nations may have conferred on Israel the credentials of nationhood; but its own idealism and courage, its own sacrifice and generosity, had earned the credentials of immortality. </p>\n<p>Some do not agree. Three weeks ago I said in a public statement: &#8220;Israel is here to stay.&#8221; The next day I was attacked by Cairo radio, rebuking me for my faith in Israel&#8230;. and&#8230;</p>\n<p>&#8230;.my flat prediction that Israel is here to stay. </p>\n<p>For Israel was not created in order to disappear &#8211; Israel will endure and flourish. </p>\n<p><strong>It is the child of hope and the home of the brave. It can neither be broken by adversity nor demoralized by success. It carries the shield of democracy and it honors the sword of freedom; and no area of the world has ever had an overabundance of democracy and freedom.</strong></p>\n\t\t\t\t</div><!-- .comment-content -->\n\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t</article><!-- .comment-body -->\n</li><!-- #comment-## -->\n</ol><!-- .children -->\n</li><!-- #comment-## -->\n</ol><!-- .children -->\n</li><!-- #comment-## -->\n\t\t<li id=\"comment-947981\" class=\"comment even thread-even depth-1 parent\">\n\t\t\t<article id=\"div-comment-947981\" class=\"comment-body\">\n\t\t\t\t<footer class=\"comment-meta\">\n\t\t\t\t\t<div class=\"comment-author vcard\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t<img alt='' src='https://secure.gravatar.com/avatar/3d19a897daa82b6f3881c43d12246fb8?s=60&#038;d=mm&#038;r=pg' srcset='https://secure.gravatar.com/avatar/3d19a897daa82b6f3881c43d12246fb8?s=120&amp;d=mm&amp;r=pg 2x' class='avatar avatar-60 photo' height='60' width='60'/>\t\t\t\t\t\t<b class=\"fn\">Mike</b> <span class=\"says\">says:</span>\t\t\t\t\t</div><!-- .comment-author -->\n\n\t\t\t\t\t<div class=\"comment-metadata\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t<a href=\"https://www.darkmoon.me/2017/under-the-heel-of-the-rothschilds/#comment-947981\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<time datetime=\"2017-02-26T20:47:33+00:00\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\tFebruary 26, 2017 at 8:47 pm\t\t\t\t\t\t\t</time>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t</a>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t</div><!-- .comment-metadata -->\n\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t</footer><!-- .comment-meta -->\n\n\t\t\t\t<div class=\"comment-content\">\n\t\t\t\t\t<p>I&#8217;d just like to point out that  the Old Testament, is believed to have been  written  on the orders of King Josiah of Judah? in about 1500 BC ? Supposedly, the Torah was (conveniently) found in a temple store room while cleaning up.  Apparently, they cleaned up every few centuries whether they needed to or not. class=\"comment-content\">\n\t\t\t\t\t<p>JFK and a &#8216;soup&#8217; of drugs&#8230;</p>\n<p>As president, he was famous for having a bad back, and since his death, biographers have pieced together details of other illnesses, including persistent digestive problems and Addison&#8217;s disease, a life-threatening lack of adrenal function.</p>\n<p>But newly disclosed medical files covering the last eight years of Kennedy&#8217;s life, including X-rays and prescription records, show that he took painkillers, antianxiety agents, stimulants and sleeping pills, as well as hormones to keep him alive, with extra doses in times of stress.</p>\n<p>At times the president took as many as eight medications a day, says the historian, Robert Dallek. A committee of three longtime Kennedy family associates, who for decades refused all requests to look at the records, granted Mr. Dallek&#8217;s, in part because of his &#8221;tremendous reputation,&#8221; said one of them, Theodore C. Sorensen, who was the president&#8217;s special counsel.</p>\n<p><a href=\"http://www.nytimes.com/2002/11/17/us/in-jfk-file-hidden-illness-pain-and-pills.html\" rel=\"nofollow\">http://www.nytimes.com/2002/11/17/us/in-jfk-file-hidden-illness-pain-and-pills.html</a></p>\n\t\t\t\t</div><!-- .comment-content -->\n\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t</article><!-- .comment-body -->\n</li><!-- #comment-## -->\n</ol><!-- .children -->\n</li><!-- #comment-## -->\n</ol><!-- .children -->\n</li><!-- #comment-## -->\n\t\t<li id=\"comment-948174\" class=\"comment even thread-even depth-1\">\n\t\t\t<article id=\"div-comment-948174\" class=\"comment-body\">\n\t\t\t\t<footer class=\"comment-meta\">\n\t\t\t\t\t<div class=\"comment-author vcard\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t<img alt='' src='https://secure.gravatar.com/avatar/ccfb36caf537432302faad377f0b2982?s=60&#038;d=mm&#038;r=pg' srcset='https://secure.gravatar.com/avatar/ccfb36caf537432302faad377f0b2982?s=120&amp;d=mm&amp;r=pg 2x' class='avatar avatar-60 photo' height='60' width='60'/>\t\t\t\t\t\t<b class=\"fn\">jerry</b> <span class=\"says\">says:</span>\t\t\t\t\t</div><!-- .comment-author -->\n\n\t\t\t\t\t<div class=\"comment-metadata\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t<a href=\"https://www.darkmoon.me/2017/under-the-heel-of-the-rothschilds/#comment-948174\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<time datetime=\"2017-03-01T01:34:43+00:00\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\tMarch 1, 2017 at 1:34 am\t\t\t\t\t\t\t</time>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t</a>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t</div><!-- .comment-metadata -->\n\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t</footer><!-- .comment-meta -->\n\n\t\t\t\t<div class=\"comment-content\">\n\t\t\t\t\t<p>Over at <a href=\"http://www.ourfintieworld.com\" rel=\"nofollow\">http://www.ourfintieworld.com</a> one will find many amusing comments and a wealth of knowledge like for example this from a CTG</p>\n<p>Myth busters<br/>\n =============<br/>\n ** When TSHTF, the elites will go to bunkers and emerge after the dust has settled and they will be the masters of earth</p>\n<p>1. America\u2019s rapidly deteriorating condition of the late seventies is what led to my search for what happened to the promise of \u201cthe American dream\u201d.\n\n\n\nWhat I cannot comprehend is all this wringing of hands, rending of garments and gnashing of teeth. By the turn of that century, they virtually owned, and most certainly controlled Britain, the sole superpower of the day, a global power on whose colonial holdings \u201cthe sun never set.\u201d\n\nThe Rothschilds also exercised considerable influence over the outcome of the Napoleonic wars (1803-1815) that served to strangle the rise of another potential superpower: France. The financial power of the Rothschilds had originally been based in France, but when Napoleon began to resist their economic plans for his country, the Rothschilds diverted money to Britain and stirred up conflict between Britain and its traditional enemy France. The result: the demise of Napoleonic power at the battle of Waterloo (1815).\n\nFrom that point on, Rothschild power grew by leaps and bounds. They played a critical part in fomenting and influencing the American revolution (1765-1783), the war of 1812 between America and Britain, the Mexican-American war of the late 1840s, and the American \u201cCivil War\u201d of 1861-1865.\n\nBy this time, the Rothschilds had begun expanding their parasitical power base to the \u201cNew world.\u201d These wars reflected their emerging interest in America and their gradual abandonment of Britain as their center of power. With the Jews it has always been about war, war, war and more war. Since the day Jews fabricated their Torah, it\u2019s always been about bloody war.\n\nBy the end of the 19th century, the Rothschilds had begun consolidating their control over America. Around the same time, a small portion of their global plan was unveiled by the sensational publication of the Protocols of the Elders of Zion (1903), since conveniently dismissed as a \u201cforgery\u201d.\n\nA scant twelve years after the new century began, the Rothschilds\u2019 full economic control over America was finally accomplished with the enactment of the Federal Reserve Act (December 1913). Within seven months of that Act, the world was at war, dragging America (with its massive army of two million troops) into the bloodshed. This was in April, 1917.\n\nThe Federal Reserve act was the very same Br\u2019er Rabbit scheme replayed with Trump\u2019s election.\n\nJewish economic influence then fomented two of the most murderous wars in history, first one in 1914 and then a second in 1939, a scant quarter of a century after the first major killing campaign. From the very beginning of the century, brush wars raged throughout the century in places like the Philippines and South America.\n\nIn spite of this headline in a major newspaper in March 1933, you will still hear Jews hotly deny that they had anything to do with starting WWII. Out of 442 US billionaires, 105 were Jews. (Source). With such enormous wealth concentrated in the hands of American Jews, is it any wonder they own the mass media and major corporations as well as have huge reserves left over for the bribery and corruption of American politicians?
